(April 25th) The Post Office Is Not Allowed to Deliver Narcotics The Anti-Smoking Association and the Ministries of Foreign Affairs and Finance Agreed on Measures The Central Anti-Smoking Committee, in order to prevent the use of mail to privately transport narcotics or instruments exclusively for taking narcotics, specially invited representatives from the Ministries of Transportation, Foreign Affairs, and Finance to hold a joint meeting in the meeting hall of the committee at 9:00 AM yesterday. The attendees included Long Dafu, representative of the Ministry of Transportation, Qian Tianren, representative of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Xu Shouzhi, representative of the Ministry of Finance, Zhong Ketuo, member of the Anti-Smoking Committee and Director of the Investigation Department, Song Zhefu, Section Chief, etc. Chairman Zhong Ketuo reported the main points of the meeting and then began to discuss inspection measures, passing a draft of 12 articles. The following are excerpts: (Article 1) In order to prevent the use of mail to privately deliver narcotics or instruments exclusively for taking narcotics, the inspection of mail shall be carried out in accordance with the provisions of these measures. (Article 2) Each of the Jianghai Customs, each parcel tax bureau, and other tax revenue agencies shall be responsible for strict inspection when parcels are taxed. If it is found that narcotics or instruments exclusively for taking narcotics are being privately delivered, they shall be immediately detained and handed over to the court together with the criminals for punishment in accordance with the law. (Article 3) After the parcel is inspected, the person in charge of the inspection shall affix an inspection seal at the seam of the inner wrapping of the parcel and affix a seal. If any traces of opening, dismantling, or resealing are found, the post office shall refuse to deliver it. (Article 4) All imported parcels, no matter where they are sent from at home or abroad, shall be opened and inspected on the spot by the customs or tax bureau when the recipient picks them up. If it is found that narcotics or instruments exclusively for taking narcotics are being privately delivered, they shall be immediately detained and handed over to the court together with the criminals for punishment in accordance with the law. (Article 5) Anti-smoking agencies may send personnel to jointly inspect the private delivery of narcotics or instruments exclusively for taking narcotics with personnel from the Jianghai Customs, each parcel tax bureau, and other tax revenue agencies, but shall not interfere with other matters. (Article 6) All import and export

Page 10

mail, in addition to parcels with special provisions, if there is suspicion of privately delivering narcotics or instruments exclusively for taking narcotics, the post office may send it to the customs tax bureau for inspection. (Article 7) If any postal agency staff member violates or shields others from privately delivering narcotics or instruments for taking narcotics, they shall be severely punished in accordance with the law upon verification. (Article 8) When necessary, anti-smoking agencies may send personnel to jointly inspect rented mailboxes in various post offices with customs tax bureau and post office personnel, and invite the lessee to the site. (Article 9) The inspection of mail shall be carried out using the most expeditious procedures. (Article 10) When each customs office and each tax bureau seizes narcotics or instruments exclusively for taking narcotics, in addition to handing them over to the court for punishment in accordance with the law, they shall report the seizure in detail to the responsible superior, who shall forward it to the anti-smoking agency for record. (Article 11) If inspectors perform their duties conscientiously, repeatedly solve major cases, or shield corruption and malpractice, and the responsible superior discovers this or someone reports it and it is verified, they shall be rewarded or punished separately in accordance with the law. (Article 12) These measures shall be implemented from the date of submission to the Executive Yuan for approval and promulgation. A Freight Station Will Be Built on the Longhai Railway in Xuzhou Xuzhou Correspondence Qian Zongze, Director of the Longhai Railway Administration, plans to take back the land on the northern section of Zhongzheng Street to build a freight station. He went from Xuzhou to Nanjing on the 17th and returned to Xuzhou on the 19th. Regarding the construction of the freight station and the addition of branch lines, the Ministry of Railways has approved the construction of the freight station first, followed by the branch lines. More than ten representatives of businessmen, including Ding Yinzhou, Zhang Guichen, and Lan Hongtao from the East China Sea, petitioned the Ministry of Railways, the headquarters of the Second Army, the county government, and the public security bureau. On the 23rd, they visited Mr. Qian again. According to Qian's reply, the construction of the freight station is to rectify transportation and develop the business of the railway. Although the previously rented land extends for more than ten li from Erbawowo in the north to the southern end of Dama Road, only the section from Erbawowo to the northern end of Zhongzheng Street will be taken back. The larger and more orderly houses number no more than seven or eight hundred. The southern section will definitely not be used. Since the representatives have pleaded for the difficulties of businessmen and the hardship of the people, it has been decided to reduce the lively market area east of Zhongzheng North Street by 40 meters (equivalent to about 3.2 zhang of the construction scale) to avoid affecting business. A large road will be built on the south street facing east to connect to the freight station to facilitate transportation. These flexible measures require relocation within two months. The representatives of the merchants have expressed satisfaction with this. It is now reported that Mr. Qian is planning to revise the route with Chief Engineer Bira. A disturbance has been put to rest. As for the issue of building a branch line from Bayiji to Taizhuang, Mr. Qian has discussed with Chief Engineer Bira to go from Xuzhou to the eastern section of the Longhai Railway for survey on the 23rd, but the required funds are about one million yuan, which needs to be investigated by the Ministry of Railways before it can be started. In addition, a freight train with 28 cars from Xuzhou to Xinpu on the Longhai Railway was derailed by bandits at around 2:00 AM on the 21st between Caopu and Baitabu. At that time, the firepower was sufficient and it could not be stopped. The train dragged along the ground, and more than a hundred sleepers were destroyed. Many goods were overturned on the ground, but fortunately no one was injured. The Xinpu Railway Bureau sent people to repair it, and the repair was completed at around 9:00 AM on the 23rd, and the train resumed traffic. The Japanese Are Actively Developing Niuzhuang Opening Four Wharves to Resist Huludao Establishing Transportation Companies to Monopolize Trade Goods Shenyang Correspondence Yingkou, also known as Niuzhuang, was the only major port for trade in Northeast China twenty years ago. Since the Japanese developed Dalian, its trade has been taken away. As a result, the import and export of Northeast China have also been manipulated by the Japanese, which greatly hinders the development of our country's economy. The Liaoning authorities, in order to recover their rights and develop the industry of Eastern Mongolia, have been preparing last year and opened Huludao as a major port in Northeast China on April 15 this year. Upon hearing the news, the Japanese believed that it was harmful to Dalian. In addition to trying to undermine it (such as spreading rumors that the construction of Huludao port has British and French capital, and the Chinese have no ability to open the port, etc.), they are also actively developing Yingkou to resist it. For example, at the end of this month, Mantetsu opened the first, second, third, and fourth wharves in Dongniujiatun. In the future, if they are successful, they can accommodate ten giant ships. The trade goods of all wharves in Yingkou can be absorbed by them, and various undertakings related to the local area near the station will be expanded. On the one hand, Japanese shipping companies are increasing the number of voyages to Shanghai, Tianjin, Qingdao, and other places to supplement port services. On the other hand, the local Japanese consul is promoting the sales of Japanese goods and encouraging Japanese businessmen to set up more import stores. Japan's largest international transportation company in Northeast China (with a capital of 20 million) has also established a branch in Hebei, appointing Ueda as the president to compete with Chinese transportation companies, attracting cargo transportation to Jinchou and Xihuikou and other places. In the future, if it is successful, the trade industry in Yingkou will be controlled by the Japanese. The people of the country should take measures to save it. It is found that the Japanese established the Yingkou Wharf Office in Niujiatun in the winter of Meiji 43 (1910), and built wharves. Later, they expanded it year by year, investing hundreds of thousands of yuan each year. Currently, there are two locations, A and B, with a wall length of more than 4,000 feet, which can accommodate five ships of 3,000 tons. The annual import and export volume is about one million tons. The import of Japanese goods into Yingkou's various wharves was worth more than 6.39 million taels of silver in the Republic of China's 17th year. There are 2,600 Japanese expatriates in Yingkou. Shops with capital of more than one million include one bank, one oil mill, two transportation merchants, and four others. Local News

The Terrible Case of Seven Deaths Reported Yesterday

The Police Department is Strictly Pursuing the Runaway Servant

Photo of the Runaway Servant Guo Song'an Located in a Photography Studio 35

The Seven Corpses Examined Yesterday Morning

Knife Handle with Fingerprints... Submitted to Fingerprint Experts for Research

The Master Suspects... The Massacre Was Caused by Adultery

The details of the unprecedented Shanghai tragedy that occurred in the home of Guo Chunsen, a Guangxi native and former peace negotiator for the Southern Government, located at No. 1069, Lane Zhi Deli, Avenue Edward VII, Shanghai, in the early hours of the day before yesterday, in which seven family members were killed and the male servant fled with money, were reported in yesterday's newspaper. The Public Concession Police Department considers this case extremely important and is making every effort to apprehend the culprit. The following is a record of the reporter's continued investigation yesterday:

Male Servant Took His Photo With Him

Chinese and Western detectives from the Jing'an Temple Road Police Station, which has jurisdiction over the area, were eager to apprehend the culprit after the horrific murder case in the home of Guo Chunsen on Avenue Edward VII the day before yesterday. However, they did not know what the fugitive looked like, making it difficult to investigate. When asked, the master, Guo Chunsen, said that he had a photo of the male servant, Guo Song'an, hanging in the back wing, but after the tragedy, the servant had taken the photo with him when he fled.

The Runaway Servant Guo Song'an

Negative Found in Photography Studio

Subsequently, Guo Cang, Chunsen's nephew, said that the male servant, Song'an, had taken a small four-inch photo at the Nanxin Photography Studio on Jing'an Temple Road in November of last year. Upon hearing this, police detectives immediately went with Guo Cang to the Nanxin Photography Studio to check. Unexpectedly, the studio, which was founded by another Japanese person, was deeply afraid that there might be other circumstances and did not listen to the detectives. For the sake of thorough investigation, the police station immediately notified the Nanxin Photography Studio with an official letter. After receiving the letter, the studio immediately checked the negatives. Guo Chunsen and Guo Cang, the masters of the house, identified the negative, and it was indeed the male servant, Guo Song'an.

Police Distribute Photos to Apprehend the Fugitive

After obtaining the negative of the runaway male servant Guo Song'an (nickname "Guangxi Mapi"), the police station immediately instructed the Nanxin Photography Studio to print two dozen more copies and distribute them to Chinese and Western detectives in various police stations so that they could pay close attention to the case and apprehend the fugitive at any time. Our newspaper has also obtained a photo of Guo Song'an and has made a special plate to publish it. Because the police are eager to know his whereabouts, anyone who has information about his secret residence can report it to the nearest police station.

The Guo Family Moves Out Today

Our reporter, wanting to understand the underlying causes of the incident, drove to the Guo residence in Lane Zhi Deli again last night to inquire. When he arrived at the entrance of the lane, the gloomy wind made him shiver. Although this is a superstitious belief, the psychological effect of being in that place late at night was indeed unsettling. When the reporter entered the Guo residence, he saw two detectives gesticulating and talking, as if they were talking about a tiger changing its color. When asked where the master of the house was, he replied that he had already lodged with relatives at six o'clock the night before and was planning to move the whole family today.

The Court Examined the Corpses Yesterday Morning

Yesterday morning, the Special District Local Court appointed Prosecutor Guo Wei to lead clerks, forensic doctors, and others to the corpse examination site on Flandre Road by car to examine the corpses of the seven victims who were killed: (1) Guo Chunsen's wife, Guo Li; (2) daughter-in-law, Liu Yanqiu; (3) grandson, Dasheng; (4) grandson, Meisheng; (5) maid, Gui Xiang; (6) Chun Lian; and (7) cook, Guo Chao Long. They examined the wounds on each of the seven corpses, male and female, young and old, and found that they were all on the neck.

Knife Handle Fingerprints Worth Studying

The Western Head of the Jing'an Temple Police Station then reported that after the incident, he went to the Guo residence to investigate the situation. He said that at 7:30 yesterday morning, the police station received a phone call from Fu Songting reporting a major murder case in Lane Zhi Deli and immediately sent Western Detective Mike Whalen to investigate. According to reports, all the residents of the Guo family, except for the child Su Sheng, were killed. However, the male servant Guo Song'an and a maid named Chonggui were missing. He requested that warrants be issued to detain these two people for questioning or to obtain clues about the case. When he went to the Guo residence to investigate, he found three sharp knives, one a kitchen knife and two axes. One knife and one ax were stained with blood, and there were fingerprints on the knife. He has now handed them over to fingerprint experts for research. He is now bringing an ax to the court for inspection.

This Case May Have Arisen from Adultery

Guo Chunsen's eldest son, Guo Bo, then filed a lawsuit stating the names and identities of the seven people who were killed and then stated that Guo Chao Long (also known as Shao Long) was his cousin and that the runaway Guo Song'an was a distant uncle. He said that he was studying at Fudan University and lived on campus and did not often go home. He did not know how the tragedy occurred, but based on the current situation, he speculated that Song'an and Chonggui may have had an affair, and his mother did not approve of their union, so he resorted to this vicious act, killing seven people and then fleeing. He requested that the two be quickly arrested and punished according to the law.

Bodyguard He's Testimony

Witness Fu Songting testified that he was working as a bodyguard at the home of a Mr. He at No. 94, Avenue Edward VII. At 6:30 yesterday morning, because the maid was dumping the chamber pot at the door, he was also standing at the door to guard the house to prevent bandits from entering. He then saw Guo's child Su Sheng coming out of his house and crying to him, saying that everyone in his house had been killed. He then went to take a look and immediately saw someone who had been killed and reported it to the police. Prosecutor Guo obtained the testimony and determined that the seven corpses of Guo Li and others, male and female, had indeed been slashed to death by the murderer with knives and axes before death. He ordered the family members of the deceased, Guo Bo, to sign a statement and take the coffins back for burial and ordered the police to strictly apprehend the murderer and bring him to justice.

Counterfeit Money Criminals Arrested in Dance Hall

Well-dressed... Extravagant Behavior

Using Counterfeit Money... Arrested as a Result

According to the Wenhui Daily, a Chinese expatriate with American citizenship, surnamed Wu, was arrested in the dance hall of the Great Eastern Hotel last night (the 25th) for allegedly using a counterfeit 100-dollar bill from the Hong Kong Mercantile Bank. According to the police and bank officials, the arrest of this person is extremely important because this type of 100-dollar counterfeit bill is so well-made that it is almost indistinguishable from the real thing. The bank has been investigating this matter since the autumn of last year and has only now arrested one person. These counterfeit bills are all imitations of bills issued by the Hong Kong branch. The bank had instructed all branches to temporarily collect all 100-dollar genuine bills issued in Hong Kong for safekeeping to facilitate investigation. Although the counterfeit bills are well-made, there is still one flaw that is easily detectable by bank staff but not easily recognizable by the general public, so they are widely circulated. The origin of the case is that the Chinese expatriate went to the Perrier Hotel on Avenue Edward VII with a dance hostess on Thursday night and presented a counterfeit 100-dollar bill. The waiter took it to a nearby money shop to exchange it and returned with 90 dollars. The next day, the money shop notified the hotel because the bank would not exchange the bill. A Chinese staff member in the hotel knew the dance hostess and, after much investigation, obtained her whereabouts and reported it to the police, who arrested him in the dance hall of the Great Eastern Hotel at night. At the time, the defendant was still drinking with the dance hostess and two Germans at the same table. Although nothing was found on the defendant's person, two counterfeit bills were found in the dance hostess's handkerchief. When questioned about their origin, she said that she got them from a small village near Hong Kong and had only been in Shanghai for six days. He was dressed in a very fashionable Western suit, spoke English with an American accent, and claimed to live in San Francisco, so he had obtained a passport from that city. He was immediately taken to the American Concession this morning. After a detailed investigation by Prosecutor Sallards and discussions with the Consul General and Concession staff, he refused to accept the trial, so the defendant will be brought to the Special District Local Court for questioning on Monday.

Voronoff Talks About Youth Gland Results

Leaves Shanghai Tomorrow, Returns Next Year

Professor Voronoff, Director of the Experimental Surgery School and Deputy Director of the Physiological Chemistry School of Paris High School, arrived in Shanghai from France a few days ago. Voronoff is famous in the global medical community for his invention of the youth gland. By grafting the youth gland of monkeys into the human body, people can rejuvenate. According to Voronoff, since he invented this technique in 1920, he and other surgeons have achieved remarkable results. Only 8% of the operations have failed. Those who have received this gland are generally 20 years younger in spirit and energy. The effects take three months to develop. The first sensation is vigorous spirit. However, after five to eight years, the effects gradually diminish, and a new gland must be grafted, and the effects are still the same. He has performed this procedure twice on more than 100 people. However, there is no one who has had the procedure done a third time, so he cannot comment on its effectiveness. The gland grafting operation is very simple. Men only need one gland, while women need three glands: the reproductive gland, the thyroid gland, and another gland. He experimented on monkeys behind closed doors for about ten years before he dared to introduce the technique to the world. He plans to go to the United States to lecture and demonstrate this technique. He will leave Shanghai on Sunday. He has given lectures in Bombay at the invitation of the British government and in Hanoi, Saigon, and Siam at the invitation of the French government. After touring the United States, he plans to return to Paris and then come back to the East, first to Japan and then to Shanghai to lecture and demonstrate surgery. The date is scheduled for around June 1931.

Ministry of Finance Restricts Savings Business

The Ministry of Finance has strict restrictions on financial institutions conducting savings business. All banks that specialize in or concurrently conduct this business must obtain approval before they can operate, in order to protect the safety of depositors and consolidate the livelihoods of ordinary people. However, in recent years, many ordinary stores in various provinces and cities have also been falsely operating savings businesses, especially in Shanghai, where there are a wide variety of ways to do this. They have not been approved and registered, and the amount of their funds and how they are used are unknown. What they absorb is the lifeblood of the people. If there is a collapse, the number of victims would be countless. This is a matter of great importance to social security and the people's livelihood. It is our duty to thoroughly investigate and prohibit this. The Shanghai Banking Association also believes that Shanghai's merchants are competing to conduct savings business as a way to attract business, and the publicity advertisements are everywhere. It has become a trend. The actual protection is difficult to predict. The public, without understanding the content, invests deposits of tens of millions of dollars. If there is any negligence, it will harm the livelihoods of ordinary people and cause great harm. The Association has specially submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance to restrict the reckless operation of savings business. The Ministry of Finance believes that the points raised by the Association are all insightful and have requested the Shanghai Special Municipality to investigate and deal with the matter and has also sent letters to the concession authorities and the Special District Local Court to thoroughly investigate and prohibit this. It is reported that the Municipal Government has sent letters to the American and French Consuls General and the Special District Local Court and has instructed its subordinates to investigate and prohibit this.

One Kidnapper Asks to Give His Savings to His Brother

Savings Book with Over 2,000 Yuan

The Other Two Kidnappers Only Want a Good Meal

The kidnappers Chen Changgen from Yangzhou, Fan Renbao from Ningbo, and Li Lisheng from Pudong, who repeatedly committed kidnapping cases against Feng Yixiang and others, were captured by the Xinzha Police Station and sentenced to death by the former Provisional Court. Judge Cheng approved Chen Changgen's request, stating that all items stored by Chen Changgen that were not expressly confiscated in the judgment could be collected by his brother Chen Yongcai. He then ordered the detectives to escort the three prisoners to the Caohejing Prison Execution Ground. Prosecutor Wang Shixian was appointed by the Local Court as the supervising officer. Police Chief Yang Deshan and Police Sergeant Chen Xihui supervised the bailiffs Wang Jianqing, Zhu Wanyuan, Xu Guoguang, and Cai Zuoqing to the execution ground. After the judge ascended the bench, he ordered the execution. Police Chief Yang directed the executioners Gu Hanqing and Yin Dao Xu to execute the three prisoners by firing squad. The corpses were taken by the court for collection and awaiting claim.

Suspicious Conversation Between Two People

Related to the Kidnapping of a Three-Year-Old Child

Arrested by the Pengpu Security Corps

The Two Strongly Deny Being Bandits

The Fourth District Public Security Bureau of Zhabei yesterday handed over a case of conspiracy to kidnap a boy by the Second Team of the Pengpu Township Security Corps. Director Jin inquired about the case, and the plaintiff, Ms. He Zhang, from Yancheng, who lived at No. 114 Xizang Road in the Public Concession, stated that her nine-year-old daughter, Da Maotou, was holding her three-year-old grandson, Jinsheng, when they went out for a stroll on the morning of the 23rd of this month. Unexpectedly, when they were walking through the intersection of Kaifeng Road, two people suddenly rushed out, both wearing black long gowns and tall and thin figures, blocking their way and snatching the child she was holding and fleeing. Her daughter was young and panicked and did not dare to shout until they had disappeared into the distance before returning home to tell her. She immediately reported the case to the Xinzha Police Station to request an arrest. After days passed without any news, she became extremely anxious and hired people to search everywhere, hoping to get her grandson back. Yesterday, her acquaintances, Chen Maochang and Wang Xingwu, were passing by Pingjiang Bridge in Zhabei when they saw two people in front of them looking flustered and followed them. Suddenly, they heard them say, "The small bucket is not important, but the big bucket knowing is terrible." (The small bucket refers to Zhang's husband, and the big bucket refers to Zhang's husband's older brother.) Chen and Wang became even more suspicious after hearing this and followed them closely, witnessing them entering the home of the defendant Wu Tingchen. They then returned to tell her and immediately reported to the Pengpu Township Security Corps and ordered many corps members to go there. The defendant Xu Zhang's feelings were weak, and he jumped out of the window to escape but was immediately arrested. Wu was also taken to the corps and ordered to reveal the two kidnappers and hand over her grandson, but he was still evasive. Please verify. According to the testimonies of He, Chen, and others, they did see two people walking into Wu's house and talking about kidnapping Ms. He Zhang's grandson. When Wu Tingchen was questioned, he said that he was from Yancheng and ran the Changxing Tea Garden on Pingjiang Bridge. Yesterday, only his uncle Wu Huaidao and neighbor Li Sanbao came to his house to collect debts. Suddenly, the security corps arrived. The tenant Xu Zhang did not know what was happening and fled out the window. He was a law-abiding businessman and had no improper behavior. Xu Zhang also testified that he was from Yangzhou and rented a room from Wu and worked as a helper at the Wang family on Pingjiang Bridge. Last night, he saw the plaintiff Ms. He Zhang and others leading many people, each holding a handgun, storming into his house. He was extremely frightened and ran away, but there was no other reason. Director Jin verified the testimonies and believed that although Wu and others did not admit to kidnapping Zhang's grandson, there was proof from Chen and Wang that they were highly suspicious and should be taken to the bureau for questioning.

Eighteen-Year-Old Daughter Seduced and Abandoned

Wang Lincheng Accuses Zheng Xiaochu of Two Crimes

Zheng Xiaochu Has a Beautiful Wife and Concubines

Why Take a Female Waiter as a Concubine?

Defendant's Lawyer Asks for the Case to be Dismissed

Wang Lincheng yesterday hired lawyer Gu Jirong as his representative to accuse Zheng Xiaochu in the French court, claiming that Zheng Xiaochu seduced the plaintiff's daughter, Wang Gendi (18 years old), in 1927. The plaintiff later found out, and since the deed was done, he allowed her to be Zheng Xiaochu's concubine. She gave birth to a daughter last year, and the previous engagement of Gendi was terminated. They intended to live together until they grew old. Unexpectedly, Zheng Xiaochu suddenly changed his mind on March 7th of this year, feigning diligence and instructing Gendi to return to Ningbo on the pretext of abandoning her. Such circumstances show that Zheng Xiaochu has committed the crime of luring away a minor under Article 257 of the Criminal Law and the crime of abandonment under Article 310. He requested that the two crimes be investigated and that 5,000 yuan in alimony be recovered. The defendant, represented by lawyer Fei Xizhen, argued that Wang Gendi, the plaintiff's daughter, worked as a hostess in the New World in 1927. The defendant was a ticket seller for a certain opera house and went to the New World to perform, which led to him meeting Gendi. They exchanged affectionate glances. Although they often met later, there was no physical relationship. However, Gendi had repeatedly borrowed money from the defendant. Although the defendant had lent her some money, there was never a close relationship. Unexpectedly, when the defendant returned to Shanghai from Qingdao last year, Wang Gendi and her mother came to the defendant's place and falsely claimed that Gendi was pregnant and falsely accused the defendant of being the father. At that time, the defendant was surprised and had a slight dispute and then left. Since then, there has been little communication. The defendant has a beautiful wife and concubines who are present in court, so why would he take a female waiter as a concubine? The law cited by the plaintiff's lawyer is not only inapplicable but also ridiculous in this case. The defendant did not fall in love with Gendi, so how can the crime of luring away a minor be established? The crime of abandonment is even more absurd. Since there was no formal marriage contract, how can this article of law be applied? The accusation is without evidence, and the lawyer requested that the case be dismissed. Judge Zhu asked Wang Gendi, "Have you ever lived with the defendant?" Wang Gendi replied, "The woman has never worked as a female waiter in the New World. The first time I was in a room with the defendant was at the Anle Palace Hotel. Later, the defendant came with his concubine to pick me up and lived in his concubine's house for several days before he drove me home." Judge Cheng ordered everyone to leave and await judgment.

Rampant Banditry in the Interior

Cocoon Merchants Prepare for Trouble

Petition the National Government for Protection

Discuss Insurance Measures

The spring silkworms in various parts of Jiangsu and Zhejiang are about to have their third sleep, and the late ones have already had their second sleep. All the funds for purchasing cocoons from local silk cocoon merchants must be prepared in advance. However, due to the unrest in various counties in the interior, foreign insurance companies have increased the premiums for various types of insurance for cocoon funds, including water, fire, theft, war, and banditry, to about double the original amount. The premium discount is too large, and the silk cocoon industry is difficult to accept. The procedures for protecting the cocoon market in various regions have been submitted to the National Government's military and civilian departments by the silk cocoon industry association, requesting that military police be dispatched to each county's cocoon market to be responsible for effective protection. For the transportation of silver, there are shallow-water gunboats and师船枪划 on the waterways, and armed military police accompany the escort on the land routes to prevent bandits from taking advantage of any opportunities. It is found that the special chapters for insurance companies to underwrite cocoon funds were established in the 16th year of Guangxu in the late Qing Dynasty. More than 50 years have passed, and the situation has changed greatly. It is necessary to renegotiate the standards for insurance premiums and insurance chapters in order to comply with them. The Shanghai Silk Factory Association has received a reply from the foreign insurance companies, scheduling a board meeting at 10:00 a.m. on the 28th of this month (Monday) at No. 17 The Bund, i.e., the building above the North China Daily News, requesting representatives to attend and discuss a proper plan for mutual compliance. The silk factory association has publicly elected Shen Huachen, Zhu Jing'an, and Wu Shenbo, three standing committee members, to attend the meeting on the scheduled date to discuss a proper plan for mutual compliance.

Zhabei Water Problem

Municipal Government Stipulates Measures

Three Bureaus Jointly Issue a Proclamation

Regarding the dispute over water meter installation in Zhabei, since the Municipal Government, the Municipal Party Department, and various parties involved have discussed four measures, a small number of property owners still hold different opinions. In order to avoid water outages, the Municipal Public Security, Social Affairs, and Public Utilities Bureaus have jointly issued the following proclamation: Regarding the joint issuance of a proclamation, the Zhabei water meter installation dispute has been discussed and agreed upon by the Municipal Government, the Party Department, and relevant parties, and four compromise measures have been announced and implemented. However, a small number of property owners still hold different opinions and have not paid the water bills owed to the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, which often leads to water outages or litigation. The Bureaus have now received an order from the Municipal Government that if there are property owners who owe water bills and are involved in litigation, before a resolution is reached, the tenants should deduct the rent and hand it over to the Public Security Bureau for safekeeping, and the water company should continue to supply water as usual. As for the implementation measures: (1) The Public Security Bureau will order the tenants to hand over the rent to the Bureau within a time limit. If they fail to do so, the Bureau will send police to collect it on their behalf. If they still delay, the water company will be allowed to stop the supply. (2) If the tenant fails to pay the rent due (except for cases where the rent increase dispute has not been resolved) for two months, the property owner may apply to the district office to send police to assist in the collection. If they fail to pay for three months, the property owner may apply to the district office to order the resident to move out, but the property owner must not use stopping the water supply as a threat. It is hereby jointly announced that, in the future, if tenants encounter property owners who owe water bills and are involved in litigation with the water company, or if property owners encounter tenants who owe rent, they should follow the aforementioned measures stipulated by the Municipal Government and must not violate them. This proclamation is issued to ensure that flammable items are stored properly to prevent fires.

Public Security Bureau Proclaims to Prevent Fires

The Municipal Public Security Bureau issued a proclamation yesterday, stating: Regarding the matter of the Shanghai South District Fire Department reporting that Xia Qi, the director of the West District, reported that on the 15th of this month, the Gan family at No. 4 Ankang Lane, Caojia Lane, was negligent, causing a fire that burned down the entire three-story building, injuring two men and women and killing three people. After a detailed inspection, it was found that a large number of films were stored upstairs and downstairs. The fire was caused by the films. Because the original quality of the films is similar to rosin, it is easy to catch fire, and the breath is very 民渐利害, which affects the sense of smell and causes abnormal depression in the brain. It can be seen that the three members of the Zhang surname family were suffocated by the breath, resulting in this tragedy. It is believed that this type of chemical substance similar to rosin is easy to catch fire, and a slight carelessness can cause great harm. It is requested to strictly prohibit this in order to protect public safety. After investigating the reports of the Department, it is found that what they saw is true. In addition to issuing a notice to subordinates and instructing them to be aware, it is also necessary to issue a proclamation to all citizens to inform them that, in the future, these dangerous items that are easy to burn should be stored carefully to prevent accidents from occurring. All must abide by this.

Ferry Overturns Outside Wusong

Twenty-Six People Rescued

Three People Not Yet Recovered

A ferry owned by Zhang Sanlang, carrying 29 men and women passengers, overturned in the waters of Xiangjian Port outside Wusong at around 8:30 a.m. yesterday. When it passed through the area, it suddenly encountered a hurricane followed by a huge wave. The ferry lost its ability to navigate and overturned. All the passengers fell into the water and cried for help on the sea. Fortunately, water police and patrol boats of the anti-smuggling camp were stationed nearby and rushed to the scene to rescue them after hearing the cries. Twenty-six men and women passengers, including Xu Changshun, Bao Qiuyan, and Jin Fan, had not ingested much water and were fortunate enough to survive. However, three people were still missing and could not be found after a thorough search. They are presumed to have joined the water god. Efforts are now being made to recover their bodies.

Fierce Debate in Japanese Parliament 61

Opposition Generals Display Their Eloquence

Almost Making the Government Unable to Answer

Dentsu, Tokyo, 26th The House of Peers continued to hold its main meeting this morning. After deliberating on the law to prevent theft, it entered the question and answer session. The House of Representatives did not hold a meeting in the afternoon because of the Cherry Blossom Viewing Meeting. In the main meeting the day after tomorrow, Ozaki Yukio will be at the forefront, attacking the government. Whether it is Oyama Ikuo, the communist general who won the seat with public expectations, other aspects also hope that his questioning speech will take the unemployment problem and the police law to the stage, and wield his spicy and passionate debate.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 26th In the question and answer battle of the plenary session of the House of Peers on the 25th, Tokubo Kishichi, an elder of the Seiyukai, stood at the forefront and raised the issue of Minister of Education Kobyashi. After questioning the Prime Minister, the Prime Minister immediately took the stage and said that Mr. Tokubo regarded the Kobyashi issue as the same as the Ohkuma incident. In fact, although the two incidents seem similar in form, their contents are completely different. The Ohkuma incident occurred during the Ohkuma Cabinet, while the Kobyashi issue arose during the previous cabinet and has nothing to do with the current cabinet. Moreover, although the preliminary trial of Kobyashi's matter has been decided, it is still before the public trial. It is unreasonable to give him responsibility. As for the matter related to Kobyashi, no one knew about it at the time of the formation of the cabinet, and I knew nothing about it at all. He sang his responsibility avoidance theory. Tokubo believed that he was not satisfied and took the stage again, saying that the Prime Minister's answer was an irresponsible answer, which was surprising. The Minister of Education of the Minister of Education's Office has caused a criminal defendant incident, which is an unprecedented ominous event. The Prime Minister wanted to use clever words to shirk his responsibility, covering up the eyes and ears of the world with one hand, which is not advisable for the Prime Minister. If such issues are taken lightly, what is the meaning of cleaning up discipline? From the perspective of the issue of discipline, question the Prime Minister's responsibility, saying thousands of words, blaming the Prime Minister for being shameless, and the Prime Minister only answered that the answer has been exhausted before, and remained silent. Then, Takegoshi Yosaburo took the stage and questioned the Minister of Finance on the issue of the gold standard. The Minister of Finance stood up and said that in order to restore the financial world, there is no other way than the gold standard. In order to reverse the trade deficit, there is no other way than for the people of the country to practice frugality. He also cited detailed figures to strongly support the austerity policy. Takegoshi reserved the right to ask questions again and adjourned the meeting. However, Tokubo's theory of the Prime Minister's responsibility made the Prime Minister quite embarrassed.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 26th In the plenary session of the House of Representatives on the 25th, after the speeches of the three ministers, including Prime Minister Hamaguchi, were completed at 4 pm, the questioning began. Chairman Fujisawa introduced Inukai, the president of the Seiyukai, to take the stage. The whole audience was silent. Mr. Inukai said that the 70% claim is the unanimous claim of Japanese naval experts, who believe that it is the minimum limit of national defense. However, Prime Minister Hamaguchi and Foreign Minister Shidehara recognized the compromise reached in London as appropriate and publicly stated that this is sufficient national defense, while the Chief of Naval Staff stated that he could not bear the responsibility of the current national defense (the applause of the Seiyukai was thunderous). The government said that the surplus financial resources generated by the military reduction will be used for tax reduction, but according to the explanation of the Foreign Minister, this agreement is a short-term agreement until 1936. After this year, Japan has to build ships to implement the 70% claim. If this is the case, then the surplus financial resources of the military reduction are temporary financial resources, and there is absolutely no way to carry out permanent tax reduction with temporary financial resources. Is this not the government's deceptive policy? (The financial and people's parties exchanged harsh words, and the parliament was in turmoil.) Inukai further criticized the government's various policies and finally mentioned the issue of Minister of Education Kobyashi's奏請, saying that this will be questioned by Mr. Ozaki Yukio. Inukai stepped down, Prime Minister Hamaguchi took the stage to answer, saying that Mr. Inukai said that as a result of the London Treaty, the guarantee of national defense could not be obtained. This is Mr. Inukai's personal arbitrary decision (the voice of漫骂 from the財政友會 never stopped). The Prime Minister's speech on the stage could not thoroughly議場. Then the parliament was slightly quiet. The Prime Minister refuted each point of Mr. Inukai's attack and stepped down. There were several back-and-forth questions and answers between the two, all with整然 reasons, presenting a magnificent view of two tigers fighting. The listening audience was greatly satisfied. Then the parliament announced a休憩. Not long after, it reopened. Ichiro Hatoyama of the Seiyukai took the stage and first attacked the Prime Minister, saying that the Prime Minister signed the London Treaty regardless of the opposition of the Chief of Naval Staff, which infringed upon the right of command and blamed him for improper measures. He then listed the facts of election interference and attacked Interior Minister Adachi and stepped down. Prime Minister Hamaguchi took the stage and said that Mr. Hatoyama pointed out the government's internal disunity on military reduction. This is based on Mr. Hatoyama's hypothetical judgment and is not the fact at all. Then Interior Minister Adachi took the stage and said that Mr. Hatoyama has repeatedly said that the government interfered in the election. In fact, the government has always respected freedom of speech. Any improper behavior, regardless of party, will be severely punished. This is unanimously recognized by the various speech agencies. He launched a counterattack against Hatoyama's attack and questions. After that, there were several simple disputes between the two over (interference) and (non-interference). At 4:40 pm, the remaining agenda was postponed. Chairman Fujisawa announced the adjournment of the meeting.

Reuters, Tokyo, 26th Newspapers carried an anonymous naval figure's paper, criticizing Foreign Minister Baron Shidehara's speech in Parliament yesterday, saying that Shidehara deliberately misinterpreted the impact of the London Naval Treaty on Japanese defense and falsely claimed that he had fully considered the opinions of naval personnel before accepting the treaty, which was tantamount to deceiving oneself and others. The newspapers also carried the news that Admiral Kato was about to resign to express his opposition to the signing of the London Naval Treaty, but this statement cannot be verified yet.

Sluggish Transactions in British Shipbuilding Industry 64

Reuters, London, 26th According to the report issued by the Shipbuilding Industry Association today, the first quarter before the end of March this year was a bad era for the British shipbuilding industry in recent years. British shipyards did not receive any transaction orders in this quarter, accounting for 50%. No one ordered cargo ships or oil tankers. The warship projects in private shipyards are now only half of what they were a year ago. Most of the crew members who were under construction at the end of March have completed their work. The future prospects of the shipbuilding industry are bleak.

Last Week's U.S. Cotton Weakened and Recovered 71

Cotton Field Estimates Reduced by Approximately 2.6 Percent

A New York dispatch on the cotton market for the past week reports: The cotton market initially weakened due to profit-taking by longs, but soon rebounded due to short covering. There are reports of continued drought in West Texas, leading to significant buying interest in new crop futures for all months. Other than that, the weather conditions are generally satisfactory. According to a local expert, cotton field estimates are reduced by approximately 2.6 percent. It is also estimated that 78 percent of cotton fields have been planted, compared to 83 percent last year. The New York Cotton Exchange estimates that total cotton stocks (including linters) as of March 31 were 7,036,000 bales, compared to 5,740,000 bales at the same time last year. Zhabei: Yesterday's supply was very scarce, around the 10th grade or so. Sales were extremely dull. Northern粳 rice especially was sluggish in movement. Except for high-grade 粳 rice, medium and lower grades were soft. Boiled rice with high price was tired, arrivals were weak, and transactions were few. The arrival of Yangdu rice boats was lacking, and stocks were depleted, making the rice market very quiet. Prices were barely stable. Currently, the market's imports and exports are mostly from factories' and warehouses' existing stocks. The white yuan buyers are not interested in accumulating goods. The market is downstream. High-grade goods opened at $18.34.

Yesterday, the market fell sharply, especially for the current month's delivery. Foreign wheat prices dropped by $0.45, and sales were extremely sluggish. If prices did not fall, they would have to deliver physical goods, further pressuring the market. The market had already lost its ability to resist. For distant months, such as May and June, it was rumored that 阜豐 released a lot of positions. With the sunny weather and declining market sentiment, prices frequently dropped. Observing the subsequent steps, if the weather does not change, the longs' misfortune may begin from here. Art World

Thomas Mann and the Buddenbrooks 85

Ming

Among Thomas Mann's three most famous works, ("Buddenbrooks") (Die Buddenbrooks), ("The Magic Mountain") (Der Zauberberg), and ("Death in Venice") (Der Tod in Venedig), ("Buddenbrooks") is considered his greatest work. This masterpiece has been hailed by critics as the pinnacle of German naturalistic literature, believing that its rich content and perfect structure are truly rare in modern literature. Not only can the author join the ranks of the world's great writers because of this novel, but the modern German literary scene can be proud even if it only produced this one work. Of course, this is the height of praise, but it is not an exaggeration, because ("Buddenbrooks") is such a book. However, we must know that it is not Mann's late work, but his first novel in his early years. When this novel was published in Germany, he was only twenty-seven years old, but he started writing it several years earlier. A young man in his twenties completed such a great and mature work, which truly makes people marvel at his flourishing talent.

The history of Mann's creation of this novel is as follows: Mann went to Munich at the age of eighteen and worked as an unpaid junior clerk in a fire insurance company. That was the beginning of his literary career, because he stole time there to write a novel called ("The Fallen"), which was later published in a magazine. This novel attracted the attention of readers, so Mann left the fire insurance company and went to Munich University to study, hoping to pursue a career in journalism in the future. But later, he followed his brother Heinrich to Italy. His brother was then a young man studying art (now also a famous writer). They lived together on Argentine Street in Rome. During this period, Mann worked hard to study literature and read many foreign writers' works. He liked Tolstoy the most. On the one hand, he naturally worked hard to create. He wrote short stories and a very long novel. So, when he returned to Munich from Italy, he brought with him the unfinished manuscript of ("Buddenbrooks"). This manuscript was started in Rome and completed in Munich. But before this work was published, he first published a collection of short stories, ("Little Mr. Friedemann") (Der Cleine Herr Friedemann). These novels, written in a fluent and natural style, made readers feel his uniqueness, thus attracting some attention. These novels were also written in Italy, but although they had little of the flavor of southern Europe, they had a strong Scandinavian mood. At this time, Mann wrote many short stories and published them in various famous German literary journals, thus gradually becoming famous. At that time, a writer visited him at his home and saw him writing the last few pages of ("Buddenbrooks") beside a Pleyel piano and under a portrait of Tolstoy. Mann read a page from his manuscript to his visitor, who was greatly impressed.

This very thick manuscript was later sent to the famous Berlin publisher Fischer, but after waiting anxiously for a long time, the bookstore still did not give him a reply. He became impatient. Coincidentally, a soldier-turned-writer, Kurt Martens, advised him to join the army. Mann followed his advice, but he could not get used to being a soldier. The hardship of training and the anxiety of waiting for a reply from the bookstore made him fall ill. When the reply from the bookstore came, he was already lying sick in bed. The bookstore's letter was very brief. The novel was too long ("Cut the wedge section shorter so that it can be printed into a book"). Mann sent back a very short reply, the gist of which was ("Either two volumes or none at all"). So the bookstore had to agree and publish the novel in two volumes.

("Buddenbrooks") built Mann's reputation in the literary world as soon as it was published. Soon it spread throughout Europe. In Germany, it has long become a must-have book for every family. (Next time, I will publish a brief description of ("Buddenbrooks"))

Notice to Aspiring Artists 86

By Yamamoto Kanae

Translated by Chen Baoyi

This is quite a difficult question.

There are no specifically required mental preparations for those aspiring to become artists. It's similar to those aspiring to be doctors, lawyers, soldiers, or merchants; the necessary mental preparations are much the same.

If I were to force the issue, I could only say that the life of an artist is inherently unprofitable, so one must be prepared for poverty. Even in France, where there are many art lovers, there is a proverb:

It says, "When a painter emerges, the family fortune declines." This is indeed true. Therefore, it is no wonder that fathers, elder brothers, and uncles who worry about their children's future strongly oppose them becoming art students. I have often seen many young people aspiring to be artists come to me for advice, but I always say, "If it's for entertainment, that's excellent. But if you want to be a professional, I don't approve," and I dissuade them.

What does poverty matter? It exists in any circumstance. However, when I think of the fierce competition for survival in this harsh, utilitarian society, I want to dissuade them. Also, having personally experienced the difficulties of art, I don't want them to enter the art world so lightly. Originally, there are too many artists in Japan now. There are too many artists, and on the other hand, there are many people who don't understand art, so they are in a predicament. However, the time will undoubtedly come when the public's appreciation of art increases, leading to the elimination of pseudo-artists. Although there are not as many art students as literature students, in almost every village, there is at least one young person with a three-legged stool. If they get selected even once for an exhibition in Tokyo, they immediately start a works distribution meeting (Translator's note: A works distribution meeting, also known as a painting association, is where artists temporarily set prices and sell paintings through reservations for a certain period). If the result is successful, they act like art students and want to become professionals. Compared to our student days, today's youth have a much stronger sense of utilitarianism, and their use of wisdom is much more calculating.

To suit the nature of an artist, first, one must be sensitive and optimistic. One's physical strength must be as strong as a soldier, yet one must have a tranquil nature. Because the life of an artist is ultimately about "seeing" and "doing," it can be said that those who have liked to watch and create since childhood are suitable to be artists. According to this, I am probably not suitable. I have heard that I used to like to watch, but I didn't really like to draw.

I remember asking my mother at some point whether she saw any sign of me becoming a painter since I was a child. But according to my mother's recollection, she said she didn't see anything like that. I heard that as a child, I liked to play with kite strings, concentrating on tying long strings and short strings together. My becoming an artist was due to studying Western woodblock engraving during my youth. It was not easy to carve out the drawings done by others, such as the plate bottoms drawn by painters like Watanabe Fumio and Ishikawa Toraji, using tens of thousands of triangular knife lines. But the result of printing it was that the interest in the plate was more evident than the interest in the painting. Although I was a child, I felt no interest in reproductive engraving, and I was thinking of becoming a painter like Fumio or Ishikawa, which was the beginning of my becoming a painter. From then on, I practiced pencil drawing on Sundays or at night. When I was twenty-one years old, I took the opportunity to be exempted from conscription and applied to art school. Actually, I barely got in at the bottom of the list. As for the things in the art school student era, let's talk about it some other time. According to my own experience, even if one graduates from art school, one still doesn't understand anything about painting.

However, even today, the Tokyo Art School is still a relatively convenient place for art students to study. Although there are four or five research institutes in Tokyo where self-taught people conduct research freely, there is no specific academic style. Although the names of great masters are posted as directors and teachers, direct guidance is extremely rare. Therefore, training as a professional is very unreliable.

In short, I believe that anyone aspiring to art must learn from a reliable master, work diligently, read widely, and have the composure to add bones and flesh to their work. Even if someone has latent genius, it won't work if their training is disorganized. Those who are easily bored will not succeed. Like my younger cousin, the deceased Murayama Kaita, although he was outstanding among the art students I directly taught, his excessive passion caused his special talent not to develop fully and led to his early death. I feel that no matter what, anything called creation must be done with the approach of architecture.

Japanese painter Nakagawa Kigen is holding a solo exhibition at the Horai Japanese Club today.

Stories of World Literature (1)(4)(6) by John Macy, translated by Hu Zhongchi 87

Chapter 38: Prose of 19th Century France

(Madame Bovary) Why is it Flaubert's best-known work? It's hard to explain fully. Why? Because (Sentimental Education) is a tragedy of youth's withering hopes, a great book. Flaubert's vision is extremely broad. He sweeps away the differences between past and present, fact and fantasy, Romanticism and Realism. In (Salammbo), he seeks color from the past, like Romantic novelists, Scott or Dumas. However, he maintains the attitude of an objective, scientific researcher. He finds tragedy in simplicity, satire in gentleness, passion in ordinariness, and the present in the past. This kind of genius is not the genius of irony and contradiction, but the genius of seeing life's wisdom as a whole. As he approached the end of his life, a cynical spirit clouded him. In the unfinished Bouvard et Pécuchet, he borrowed small figures from the countryside and described all of humanity as fools. This aristocratic hater of the ordinary ultimately regarded us all as ordinary. Flaubert incorporated reason into romance, transforming the facts of life into exquisite beauty. Truth is not monotonous, and the elegance of words lies in simplicity, precision, clarity, and logic. This is a lesson that only masters can learn, and it instructs the Realism that followed him.

Maupassant, a master of the short story, is considered a disciple of Flaubert, but he did not rely on any teacher's originality. In Maupassant, nothing exists except the story, the unadorned outlines of the people who tell the story, and the place where the story happens. No writer has ever had such an interest in the problems of life's stories. It is contradictory and appropriate to put the flamboyant Romantic writer and the strict Realist together, except for Dumas. They follow separate paths, with a common gift: the ability to control all commentary about their characters. People (exist) and (act). There, human analysis, the choice between good and evil, and the contending (psychology) do not exist. Naturally, the similarities end there, because Dumas lives in a colorful past, inventing stimulating situations, while Maupassant lives in brothels and on the streets, pretending not to invent, like a Romantic falsehood that fools no one. However, the force that makes life speak for itself from within actions, without showing the appearance of manipulating human problems, Dumas has it in a different way, and Maupassant also has it within the scope of his own observations. This is a quality seen in Boccaccio and (The Arabian Nights), but often lacking in most modern novels. But if life is pitiful, comical, cruel, and vile, it seems that life, not Maupassant, should be held responsible. Why do I say this? Because Maupassant likes to depict aspects of life that are not the conventional material of parlor conversations, and some of his novels are criticized even in France, and probably should not be read by young and weak people. However, Maupassant's ethical outlook is generally sound and stern. On this point, we can trust Tolstoy. When he reached his most austere moral stage, he said, "(After Victor Hugo, Maupassant is the best modern writer. I like him very much, placing him above all his contemporaries,)" expressing that his first work showing his genius, "Boule de Suif," is a very sympathetic story, although it often seems cold on the surface. His observation of people and things is entirely for the sake of knowing what kind of stories they produce, and, regardless of whether the story is pleasant or unpleasant, he does not lean towards good or evil, towards heroes or villains, never focusing on anything other than the direct effect of his own story. He tells the story fairly and selflessly for the story itself. His language is powerful and cautious, with no superfluous matters and not a single unnecessary word. Maupassant's supreme artistry in the field of the short story makes us forget that he is a novelist with more lasting power. (A Woman's Life) and (Strong as Death) are novels that French literature can produce close to perfection.

Home
